	focus = {

		cost = 5

		available = {
			or = {

				has_completed_focus = ita_regoup_fascist
				has_completed_focus = ita_towards_republic
			}
		}

				has_government = communism

			}
		}

		}

		completion_reward = {

			air_experience = 25
			navy_experience = 25

			add_timed_idea = { idea = ITA_Navy_Plan_idea days = 365 }

			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = infantry_equipment_0
				amount = 7500
				producer = AUS
			}

			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = support_equipment
				amount = 300
				producer = AUS
			}

			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = artillery_equipment_1
				amount = 300
				producer = CZE
			}

				name = "CR.42" #

##########################################海军线##########################################
	focus = {
		id = ITA_Invest_in_naval_construction
		icon = GFX_goal_generic_construct_naval_dockyard

		prerequisite = {
			focus = ITA_Evaluate_the_army
		}

		x = 0
		y = 1

		relative_position_id = ITA_Evaluate_the_army

		cost = 5

		available = {
			any_state = {
				is_coastal = yes
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
			}
		}

		bypass = {

		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 50
		}

		available_if_capitulated = yes

		completion_reward = {

			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				prioritize = { 115 }
				limit = {
					free_building_slots = {
						building = dockyard
						size > 1
						include_locked = yes
					}
				}
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
				add_building_construction = {
					type = dockyard
					level = 2
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				prioritize = { 2 }
				limit = {
					free_building_slots = {
						building = dockyard
						size > 1

						NOT = { has_tech = basic_ship_hull_carrier }
					}
					set_technology = { basic_ship_hull_carrier = 1 }
				}

				create_equipment_variant = {
					name = "Aquila Class"
					type = ship_hull_carrier_1
					name_group = ITA_CV_HISTORICAL
					parent_version = 0
					allow_without_tech = yes #Makes no difference since focus grants appropriate tech (above), but it improves tooltip
					modules = {
						fixed_ship_deck_slot_1 = ship_deck_space
						fixed_ship_deck_slot_2 = ship_deck_space
						fixed_ship_anti_air_slot = ship_anti_air_2
						fixed_ship_radar_slot = empty
						fixed_ship_engine_slot = carrier_ship_engine_2
						fixed_ship_secondaries_slot = empty
						front_1_custom_slot = ship_deck_space
					}
				}

					equipment = {
						type = ship_hull_carrier_1

						version_name = "Aquila Class"
					}

					progress = 0.45
					amount = 1
				}
				add_equipment_production = {
					equipment = {
						type = ship_hull_carrier_1
						creator = "ITA"
						version_name = "Aquila Class"
					}
					name = "Thalassa"
					requested_factories = 5
					progress = 0.45
					amount = 1
				}
			}

			##############
			### NO MTG ###
			##############
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_tech = basic_carrier }
					}
					set_technology = { basic_carrier = 1 }
				}
				create_equipment_variant = {
					name = "Aquila Class"
					type = carrier_2
					allow_without_tech = yes #Makes no difference since focus grants appropriate tech (above), but it improves tooltip

						carrier_armor_upgrade = 2
						ship_engine_upgrade = 2
						ship_reliability_upgrade = 2
					}
				}
				add_equipment_production = {
					equipment = {
						type = carrier_2
						creator = "ITA"
						version_name = "Aquila Class"
					}
					requested_factories = 2
					progress = 0.45
					amount = 1
				}
			}
